python
import csv
import io
import json
import re

def tsv_to_jsonl(tsv_string: str, sheet_name: str = "Data") -> str:
    """
    Converts a TSV string to a JSON Lines string according to specified rules.

    Args:
        tsv_string: The input TSV data as a string.
        sheet_name: The name of the sheet to include in the JSON output.

    Returns:
        A string containing JSON objects, one per line.
    """
    tsv_file = io.StringIO(tsv_string)
    reader = csv.reader(tsv_file, delimiter='\t')

    # 1. Read the header row
    try:
        header = next(reader)
    except StopIteration:
        return "" # Empty TSV input

    # Helper function to convert string to snake_case
    def to_snake_case(name):
        name = name.strip()
        # Replace non-alphanumeric characters (except underscore) with a single underscore
        name = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9]+', '_', name)
        name = name.lower()
        # Collapse multiple underscores into one
        name = re.sub(r'_+', '_', name)
        # Remove leading/trailing underscores
        name = name.strip('_')
        return name
    
    snake_case_headers = [to_snake_case(h) for h in header]

    json_lines = []
    row_index = 1  # 1-based index for data rows

    # 2. Process data rows
    for row in reader:
        data_object = {}
        has_non_empty_field = False
        
        # Ensure row has the same number of columns as the header.
        # Pad with empty strings if the row is shorter than the header.
        # Truncate if the row is longer (though not expected for clean TSV).
        processed_row_values = row + [''] * (len(snake_case_headers) - len(row))
        processed_row_values = processed_row_values[:len(snake_case_headers)]

        for i, header_key in enumerate(snake_case_headers):
            field_value = processed_row_values[i]
            
            # Trim leading/trailing spaces
            field_value = field_value.strip()
            
            # Collapse internal newlines to a single space (and surrounding whitespace)
            field_value = re.sub(r'\s*\n\s*', ' ', field_value)
            
            # Assign value to data object. All values are treated as strings.
            data_object[header_key] = field_value
            
            # Check if this field is non-empty for the 'drop rows with all-empty columns' rule
            if field_value != "":
                has_non_empty_field = True
        
        # Drop rows with all-empty columns
        if not has_non_empty_field:
            continue

        # Construct the final JSON object for this line
        json_line = {
            "sheet": sheet_name,
            "row_index": row_index,
            "data": data_object
        }
        
        # Append the JSON object as a string, preserving non-ASCII characters
        json_lines.append(json.dumps(json_line, ensure_ascii=False))

        row_index += 1

    return "\n".join(json_lines)

# Provided TSV string

print(tsv_to_jsonl(tsv_input, sheet_name="Data"))

# Split the TSV data into lines, removing any leading/trailing empty lines
lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')

# If there's no data or only an empty header, exit
if not lines:
    exit()

# Extract the header row
header_raw = lines[0].split('\t')

# Convert header names to snake_case keys.
# "Unnamed: 0" becomes "unnamed_0", "2020" remains "2020".
keys = [h.strip().replace(':', '_').lower() for h in header_raw]

json_lines_output = []
row_index_counter = 0 # 1-based index for valid data rows

# Process data rows (starting from the second line of the TSV)
for line in lines[1:]:
    values_raw = line.split('\t')
    
    processed_values = []
    is_all_empty = True
    
    # Process each cell value in the row
    for value in values_raw:
        # Trim leading/trailing spaces and collapse internal newlines to a single space
        cleaned_value = value.strip().replace('\n', ' ')
        processed_values.append(cleaned_value)
        
        # Check if the row contains any non-empty values
        if cleaned_value:
            is_all_empty = False
            
    # Drop rows with all-empty columns (after trimming and newline collapsing)
    if is_all_empty:
        continue # Skip this row and do not increment row_index_counter

    row_index_counter += 1 # Increment for valid data rows only
    
    # Create the 'data' object by zipping keys and processed values
    # zip will handle cases where the number of values might differ from keys by truncating
    data_object = dict(zip(keys, processed_values))
    
    # Construct the final JSON object for this line
    json_line_object = {
        "sheet": "Data",
        "row_index": row_index_counter,
        "data": data_object
    }
    
    # Convert the dictionary to a JSON string and append to output list
    # ensure_ascii=False is used to preserve non-ASCII characters (like Thai) directly
    json_lines_output.append(json.dumps(json_line_object, ensure_ascii=False))

# Print each JSON object on a new line
for json_str in json_lines_output:
    print(json_str)
python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(name):
    """Converts a string to snake_case for JSON keys."""
    name = name.strip()
    if not name:
        return ""

    # Handle purely numeric names like "2020" by prepending 'col_'
    if name.isdigit():
        return f"col_{name}"

    # Replace sequences of non-alphanumeric (and non-underscore) characters with a single space
    name = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9_]+', ' ', name)
    # Convert spaces to underscores and lowercase
    name = name.replace(' ', '_').lower()
    # Remove leading/trailing underscores that might result from stripping/replacements
    name = name.strip('_')
    return name

"""

json_lines_output = []
lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')

if not lines:
    # No data to process
    exit()

# Extract and snake_case headers from the first line
header_line = lines[0]
headers_raw = header_line.split('\t')
headers_snake_case = [to_snake_case(h) for h in headers_raw]

# Process data rows starting from the second line
row_index_counter = 0
for line in lines[1:]:
    cells = line.split('\t')

    # Adjust number of cells to match headers, padding with empty strings if fewer
    if len(cells) < len(headers_snake_case):
        cells.extend([''] * (len(headers_snake_case) - len(cells)))
    # If more cells than headers, truncate to match headers (shouldn't happen with well-formed TSV)
    elif len(cells) > len(headers_snake_case):
        cells = cells[:len(headers_snake_case)]

    processed_cells = []
    for cell in cells:
        # Trim leading/trailing spaces
        cell = cell.strip()
        # Collapse internal newlines (and surrounding whitespace) to a single space
        cell = re.sub(r'\s*\n\s*', ' ', cell)
        processed_cells.append(cell)
    
    # Drop rows with all-empty columns
    if all(not cell for cell in processed_cells):
        continue

    row_index_counter += 1
    
    data_object = {}
    for i, header in enumerate(headers_snake_case):
        data_object[header] = processed_cells[i]

    json_line_obj = {
        "sheet": "Data",
        "row_index": row_index_counter,
        "data": data_object
    }
    json_lines_output.append(json.dumps(json_line_obj, ensure_ascii=False))

# Print each JSON object on a new line
for line in json_lines_output:
    print(line)

python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(name):
    """
    Converts a string to snake_case.
    - Trims leading/trailing whitespace.
    - Converts to lowercase.
    - Replaces non-alphanumeric characters (except spaces) with single spaces.
    - Replaces all whitespace with single underscores.
    - Collapses multiple underscores.
    - Removes leading/trailing underscores.
    - Prepends an underscore if the final string starts with a digit.
    """
    name = str(name).strip()
    if not name:
        return ""

    name = name.lower()
    # Replace non-alphanumeric, non-space characters with a space
    name = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]', ' ', name, flags=re.UNICODE)
    
    # Replace all sequences of whitespace with a single underscore
    name = re.sub(r'\s+', '_', name)
    
    # Collapse multiple underscores to a single one
    name = re.sub(r'_+', '_', name)
    
    # Remove leading/trailing underscores
    name = name.strip('_')

    # Prepend an underscore if the key starts with a digit to ensure it's a valid identifier in some contexts
    if name and name[0].isdigit():
        name = '_' + name
        
    return name

def tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_string, sheet_name="Data"):
    """
    Converts a TSV string to JSON Lines according to the specified rules.

    Args:
        tsv_string (str): The input TSV data.
        sheet_name (str): The name of the sheet to be included in each JSON object.

    Returns:
        str: A string containing JSON Lines, with each line being a JSON object.
    """
    json_lines = []
    
    # Strip leading/trailing whitespace from the whole TSV string and split into lines
    lines = tsv_string.strip().split('\n')

    # If the input is empty or contains only an empty header line, return empty string
    if not lines or not lines[0].strip():
        return ""

    # Extract headers from the first line and convert to snake_case
    header_raw = lines[0].split('\t')
    headers = [to_snake_case(h) for h in header_raw]
    
    # Filter out any potentially empty header names (e.g., from `to_snake_case` if input was just `!@#`)
    # and ensure there's at least one valid header.
    if not any(headers):
        return "" # No valid headers to process data against

    row_index_counter = 0

    # Process data rows starting from the second line
    for line in lines[1:]:
        # Skip completely empty lines in the data section
        if not line.strip():
            continue

        raw_values = line.split('\t')
        
        # Clean and process each cell value
        cleaned_values = []
        is_row_empty = True
        for value in raw_values:
            # Collapse internal newlines and multiple spaces to a single space, then trim leading/trailing spaces
            cleaned_value = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', value).strip()
            if cleaned_value:
                is_row_empty = False
            cleaned_values.append(cleaned_value)
        
        # Drop rows with all-empty columns (after cleaning)
        if is_row_empty:
            continue

        # Create the 'data' object for the current row
        data_object = {}
        for i, header in enumerate(headers):
            # Assign value if available, otherwise an empty string
            data_object[header] = cleaned_values[i] if i < len(cleaned_values) else ""
        
        # Increment row index for valid data rows
        row_index_counter += 1
        
        # Construct the full JSON object for the line
        json_object = {
            "sheet": sheet_name,
            "row_index": row_index_counter,
            "data": data_object
        }
        # Append the JSON object as a string, ensuring non-ASCII characters are properly handled
        json_lines.append(json.dumps(json_object, ensure_ascii=False))

    return "\n".join(json_lines)

# Convert the TSV data to JSON Lines
result = tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_data, sheet_name="Data")

python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(name):
    """
    Converts a header string to snake_case.
    Handles 'Unnamed: X' specifically and converts other headers by
    lowercasing and replacing spaces with underscores.
    """
    name = name.strip()
    
    # Specific handling for "Unnamed: X" headers (case-insensitive)
    match = re.match(r'Unnamed:\s*(\d+)', name, re.IGNORECASE)
    if match:
        return 'unnamed_' + match.group(1)

    # For other headers, convert to lowercase and replace spaces with underscores
    name = name.lower()
    # Replace one or more spaces with a single underscore
    name = re.sub(r'\s+', '_', name)
    # Remove any leading/trailing underscores that might result from processing
    name = name.strip('_')
    return name

def convert_tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_data):
    """
    Converts TSV data to JSON Lines format according to the specified rules.
    """
    lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')
    if not lines:
        return []

    headers = lines[0].split('\t')
    data_rows = lines[1:]

    # Process headers to snake_case
    snake_case_headers = [to_snake_case(h) for h in headers]

    output_json_lines = []
    row_index_counter = 0

    for row_str in data_rows:
        cells = row_str.split('\t')
        
        processed_cells = []
        all_empty_in_row = True

        for cell in cells:
            # Trim leading/trailing spaces
            trimmed_cell = cell.strip()
            
            # Collapse internal newlines to a single space
            # (Though not present in this TSV, this handles the requirement)
            collapsed_cell = ' '.join(trimmed_cell.splitlines())
            
            if collapsed_cell:
                all_empty_in_row = False
                processed_cells.append(collapsed_cell)
            else:
                # Use None for empty strings to represent JSON null
                processed_cells.append(None) 

        # Drop rows with all-empty columns
        if all_empty_in_row:
            continue

        row_index_counter += 1
        
        # Create the 'data' object
        data_object = {}
        for i, header_key in enumerate(snake_case_headers):
            # Assign value, handling cases where a row might have fewer columns than headers
            value = processed_cells[i] if i < len(processed_cells) else None
            data_object[header_key] = value

        # Construct the final JSON object
        json_object = {
            "sheet": "Data",
            "row_index": row_index_counter,
            "data": data_object
        }
        
        # Append the JSON object as a string (ensure_ascii=False for non-ASCII characters)
        output_json_lines.append(json.dumps(json_object, ensure_ascii=False))
        
    return output_json_lines

# Provided TSV data

# Convert and print the JSON Lines output
json_lines_output = convert_tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_input)

    print(line)
python
import json
import re

def clean_string(s):
    """Trims leading/trailing spaces and collapses internal newlines to a single space."""
    if s is None:
        return ""
    # Collapse internal newlines to a single space
    s = s.replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', '')
    # Trim leading/trailing spaces
    s = s.strip()
    return s

def to_snake_case(name):
    """Converts a string to snake_case, handling 'Unnamed: X' specifically."""
    name = clean_string(name)
    if not name:
        return ""
    
    # Handle specific "Unnamed: X" case
    if name.lower().startswith("unnamed:"):
        parts = name.split(":")
        if len(parts) == 2 and parts[1].strip().isdigit():
            return f"unnamed_{parts[1].strip()}"
            
    # General snake_case conversion
    # Remove non-alphanumeric characters (except spaces and underscores)
    name = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9_ ]', '', name)
    # Convert CamelCase to snake_case (e.g., FooBar -> foo_bar)
    name = re.sub(r'(.)([A-Z][a-z]+)', r'\1_\2', name)
    # Convert camelCase to snake_case (e.g., fooBar -> foo_bar)
    name = re.sub(r'([a-z0-9])([A-Z])', r'\1_\2', name)
    # Replace spaces with underscores and convert to lowercase
    name = name.replace(' ', '_').lower()
    # Collapse multiple underscores
    name = re.sub(r'_+', '_', name)
    # Remove leading/trailing underscores
    return name.strip('_')

def tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_data, sheet_name="Data"):
    """
    Converts TSV data to JSON Lines format according to specified rules.
    """
    lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')
    if not lines:
        return []

    # Extract and process header
    header_raw = lines[0].split('\t')
    header_keys = [to_snake_case(h) for h in header_raw]

    json_output_lines = []
    row_index_counter = 1

    # Process data rows
    for line in lines[1:]:
        raw_values = line.split('\t')
        cleaned_values = [clean_string(v) for v in raw_values]

        # Drop rows with all-empty columns
        if all(not v for v in cleaned_values):
            continue

        data_object = {}
        for i, key in enumerate(header_keys):
            # Assign value or empty string if column is missing/beyond data length
            data_object[key] = cleaned_values[i] if i < len(cleaned_values) else ""
        
        json_record = {
            "sheet": sheet_name,
            "row_index": row_index_counter,
            "data": data_object
        }
        json_output_lines.append(json.dumps(json_record, ensure_ascii=False))
        row_index_counter += 1

    return json_output_lines

python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(name):
    """
    Converts a string to snake_case, preserving non-ASCII characters and
    replacing common delimiters with underscores.
    """
    name = name.strip()
    name = name.lower()
    
    # Replace common delimiters/punctuation with underscores
    # This regex specifically targets common separators like spaces, colons,
    # periods, commas, hyphens, and parentheses.
    name = re.sub(r'[\s:./,()-]+', '_', name)
    
    # Collapse multiple underscores and strip leading/trailing underscores
    name = re.sub(r'_+', '_', name).strip('_')
    
    return name

def process_cell_value(value):
    """
    Trims leading/trailing spaces, collapses internal newlines to a single space,
    and attempts to convert the value to an integer, float, or returns it as a string.
    An empty string after processing is converted to None.
    """
    value = value.strip()
    value = re.sub(r'[\r\n]+', ' ', value) # Collapse internal newlines

    if value == '':
        return None

    # Try converting to int
    try:
        return int(value)
    except ValueError:
        pass

    # Try converting to float
    try:
        return float(value)
    except ValueError:
        pass

    # If not a number, return as string
    return value

def tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_string, sheet_name="Data"):
    json_lines = []
    lines = tsv_string.strip().split('\n')

    if not lines:
        return ""

    # Process header row
    header_raw = lines[0].split('\t')
    header_keys = [to_snake_case(h) for h in header_raw]

    row_index = 1
    # Iterate over data rows, starting from the second line
    for line in lines[1:]:
        cells_raw = line.split('\t')

        # Pad row with empty strings if it has fewer columns than the header
        if len(cells_raw) < len(header_keys):
            cells_raw.extend([''] * (len(header_keys) - len(cells_raw)))
        
        # Trim `cells_raw` to match the number of header keys, ignoring any extra columns
        cells_to_process = cells_raw[:len(header_keys)]

        # Process each cell value
        processed_cells = [process_cell_value(cell) for cell in cells_to_process]

        # Drop rows with all-empty columns (all values are None after processing)
        if all(val is None for val in processed_cells):
            continue

        # Create the 'data' object for the current row
        data_object = {}
        for i in range(len(header_keys)):
            data_object[header_keys[i]] = processed_cells[i]
            
        # Construct the final JSON object for the line
        json_object = {
            "sheet": sheet_name,
            "row_index": row_index,
            "data": data_object
        }
        
        # Append the JSON object as a string to the list.
        # ensure_ascii=False handles non-ASCII characters (like Thai) correctly.
        json_lines.append(json.dumps(json_object, ensure_ascii=False))
        row_index += 1

    return "\n".join(json_lines)

python
import re
import json

def to_snake_case(text):
    """
    Converts a string to snake_case, handling mixed-language characters and common separators.
    - Converts to lowercase.
    - Replaces non-alphanumeric (except Thai characters and underscores) with a single underscore.
    - Collapses multiple underscores.
    - Trims leading/trailing underscores.
    """
    if not isinstance(text, str):
        text = str(text)

    # Convert to lowercase
    s = text.lower()

    # Replace specific separators with underscores
    s = s.replace('-', '_').replace(' ', '_').replace('.', '_').replace('/', '_')

    # Keep Thai Unicode characters as alphanumeric.
    # Pattern: match anything that is NOT a letter (a-z), a digit (0-9),
    # an underscore (_), or a Thai character (\u0E00-\u0E7F).
    # Replace such matches with a single underscore.
    # This also handles parentheses.
    s = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9_\u0E00-\u0E7F]+', '_', s)
    
    # Collapse multiple underscores into one
    s = re.sub(r'_+', '_', s)
    
    # Trim leading/trailing underscores
    s = s.strip('_')
    
    return s

def tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_string):
    lines = tsv_string.strip().split('\n')
    
    # The actual header row is identified as the line starting with "ID-Emp."
    # In the given TSV, it's at index 6 (7th line).
    header_line_index = -1
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if line.startswith("ID-Emp."):
            header_line_index = i
            break
            
    if header_line_index == -1:
        # Fallback if header not found (though for this problem, it's guaranteed)
        return "" 

    # Extract column names and convert to snake_case
    raw_headers = lines[header_line_index].split('\t')
    column_names = [to_snake_case(h) for h in raw_headers]
    
    json_lines = []
    row_counter = 0
    
    # Process all lines except the first line and the identified header line
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        if i == 0 or i == header_line_index: # Skip the "Unnamed" header and the actual header row
            continue
            
        raw_cells = line.split('\t')
        
        data_obj = {}
        all_empty_columns = True
        
        # Populate data_obj with processed values
        for j, cell_value in enumerate(raw_cells):
            if j < len(column_names): # Ensure we don't go out of bounds for column_names
                processed_value = cell_value.strip().replace('\n', ' ')
                
                if processed_value: # If the value is not empty after processing
                    all_empty_columns = False
                
                # Assign to data_obj, using empty string for empty cells
                data_obj[column_names[j]] = processed_value
            # If there are more columns in data than in header, ignore them
        
        # Drop rows with all-empty columns
        if not all_empty_columns:
            row_counter += 1
            json_line_obj = {
                "sheet": "Data",
                "row_index": row_counter,
                "data": data_obj
            }
            # Use ensure_ascii=False to correctly output Thai characters
            json_lines.append(json.dumps(json_line_obj, ensure_ascii=False))
            
    return "\n".join(json_lines)

def to_snake_case(name):
    """Converts a string to snake_case, handling 'Unnamed: X' and purely numeric strings."""
    name = str(name).strip()
    # Replace 'Unnamed: X' with 'unnamed_x'
    name = re.sub(r'Unnamed: (\d+)', r'unnamed_\1', name)
    # Replace any non-alphanumeric character (except underscore) with an underscore
    name = re.sub(r'[^\w]+', '_', name)
    # Convert to lowercase
    name = name.lower()
    # Remove leading/trailing underscores
    name = name.strip('_')
    # Replace multiple underscores with a single underscore
    name = re.sub(r'_{2,}', '_', name)
    
    # If the resulting name is purely numeric (e.g., "2020"), prefix with "col_"
    if name.isdigit():
        name = "col_" + name
    return name

lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')
if not lines:
    exit()

# Extract and process headers
header_line = lines[0]
raw_headers = header_line.split('\t')
processed_headers = [to_snake_case(h) for h in raw_headers]

json_output = []
row_index_counter = 0

# Process data rows
for line in lines[1:]:
    raw_values = line.split('\t')
    
    # Clean values: trim spaces, collapse newlines to a single space
    cleaned_values = []
    for value in raw_values:
        # Collapse internal newlines to a single space
        value = value.replace('\r\n', ' ').replace('\n', ' ').replace('\r', ' ')
        # Trim leading/trailing spaces
        cleaned_values.append(value.strip())

    # Drop rows with all-empty columns
    if all(not val for val in cleaned_values):
        continue

    row_index_counter += 1
    
    # Create the data object with snake_case keys
    data_object = {}
    for i, key in enumerate(processed_headers):
        if i < len(cleaned_values):
            data_object[key] = cleaned_values[i]
        else:
            # Handle cases where a row has fewer columns than headers
            data_object[key] = ""

    # Construct the final JSON object
    json_line = {
        "sheet": "Data",
        "row_index": row_index_counter,
        "data": data_object
    }
    
    json_output.append(json.dumps(json_line, ensure_ascii=False))

for item in json_output:
    print(item)

python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(name):
    """
    Converts a string to snake_case, handling 'Unnamed: X' specifically and
    preserving non-ASCII characters that are part of words.
    """
    name = name.strip()

    # Handle 'Unnamed: X' pattern explicitly
    unnamed_match = re.match(r"Unnamed:\s*(\d+)", name, re.IGNORECASE)
    if unnamed_match:
        return f"unnamed_{unnamed_match.group(1)}"

    # Replace common separators (spaces, dots, parentheses, hyphens, colons) with a single underscore
    s = re.sub(r'[\s\.\(\)\-]+', '_', name)
    # Collapse multiple underscores to a single one
    s = re.sub(r'_+', '_', s)
    # Trim leading/trailing underscores
    s = s.strip('_')
    # Convert the entire string to lowercase
    s = s.lower()

    return s

def process_cell_value(value):
    """
    Trims leading/trailing spaces, collapses internal newlines to a single space,
    and attempts to convert the value to an integer if it meets specific criteria
    (e.g., not a phone number format). Otherwise, returns the value as a string.
    """
    value = value.strip()
    # Collapse internal newlines/carriage returns to a single space
    value = re.sub(r'[\r\n]+', ' ', value)

    if not value:
        return None  # Represent empty strings as JSON null

    # Attempt to convert to integer based on conservative rules
    # This avoids converting values that look like phone numbers or have special characters
    if value.lstrip('-').isdigit():  # Checks if it's an integer, potentially negative
        # Heuristic: if it starts with '0' (and is more than just '0'), treat as string (e.g., phone number)
        if (value.startswith('0') and len(value) > 1) or \
           (value.startswith('-0') and len(value) > 2):
            return value
        try:
            return int(value)
        except ValueError:
            pass  # Fall through to return as string

    return value

def tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_data, sheet_name="Data"):
    """
    Converts TSV data into JSON Lines format according to the specified rules.
    """
    lines = tsv_data.strip().split('\n')

    if not lines:
        return []

    # Extract and process headers from the first line
    header_line = lines[0]
    raw_headers = header_line.split('\t')
    column_names = [to_snake_case(h) for h in raw_headers]

    json_output_lines = []
    row_index_counter = 0

    # Process data rows
    for line in lines[1:]:
        raw_values = line.split('\t')

        # Ensure consistent number of columns. Pad with empty strings or truncate.
        if len(raw_values) < len(column_names):
            raw_values.extend([''] * (len(column_names) - len(raw_values)))
        elif len(raw_values) > len(column_names):
            raw_values = raw_values[:len(column_names)]

        processed_values = [process_cell_value(v) for v in raw_values]

        # Drop rows where all processed column values are None (empty)
        if all(v is None for v in processed_values):
            continue

        row_index_counter += 1
        data_object = {}
        for i, col_name in enumerate(column_names):
            data_object[col_name] = processed_values[i]

        json_line = {
            "sheet": sheet_name,
            "row_index": row_index_counter,
            "data": data_object
        }
        json_output_lines.append(json.dumps(json_line, ensure_ascii=False))
    
    return json_output_lines

python
import json
import re

def to_snake_case(text):
    """Converts a string to snake_case, handling special characters and spaces."""
    if not isinstance(text, str):
        text = str(text)
    
    # Trim leading/trailing spaces
    text = text.strip()
    
    # Replace non-alphanumeric characters (excluding spaces) with a single underscore
    # This includes characters like ':', '&', etc.
    text = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9 ]', '', text)
    
    # Replace one or more spaces with a single underscore
    text = re.sub(r'\s+', '_', text)
    
    # Convert to lowercase
    text = text.lower()
    
    # Remove any leading/trailing underscores that might have been created
    text = text.strip('_')
    
    # Collapse multiple underscores to a single underscore
    text = re.sub(r'_+', '_', text)
    
    return text

def convert_tsv_to_json_lines(tsv_string):
    """
    Converts a TSV string to JSON Lines according to the specified rules.
    """
    lines = tsv_string.strip().split('\n')
    if not lines:
        return ""

    # Parse header and convert to snake_case
    header_raw = lines[0].split('\t')
    headers_snake_case = [to_snake_case(h) for h in header_raw]

    json_output_lines = []
    # row_index is 1-based inside the chunk (referring to original data row number)
    row_index_counter = 0 

    # Process data rows
    for line in lines[1:]:
        row_index_counter += 1 # Increment for each physical data row in the input TSV
        
        cells_raw = line.split('\t')

        processed_cells = []
        all_cells_empty_after_processing = True

        for cell in cells_raw:
            # Trim leading/trailing spaces
            cell = cell.strip()
            
            # Collapse internal newlines to a single space
            cell = re.sub(r'\s*\n\s*', ' ', cell)
            
            # Check if the cell content is non-empty after processing
            if cell:
                all_cells_empty_after_processing = False
            processed_cells.append(cell)

        # Drop rows with all-empty columns (after trimming and newline collapsing)
        if all_cells_empty_after_processing:
            continue

        # Construct the 'data' object
        data_object = {}
        # Ensure that headers and cells are paired correctly, handling potential mismatches
        # For well-formed TSV, len(headers) should match len(cells)
        num_cols = min(len(headers_snake_case), len(processed_cells))
        for i in range(num_cols):
            data_object[headers_snake_case[i]] = processed_cells[i]

        # Construct the final JSON object for the line
        json_line_object = {
            "sheet": "Data",
            "row_index": row_index_counter,
            "data": data_object
        }
        
        # Append the JSON string to the output, preserving non-ASCII characters
        json_output_lines.append(json.dumps(json_line_object, ensure_ascii=False))

    return "\n".join(json_output_lines)

# Provided TSV input
